\"staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/registry/rest/create.go\", \"symbol\": \"AdmissionToValidateObjectFunc\"}\n  ],\n  \"text\": \"The Kubernetes API server admission controller pipeline is implemented across several packages in the kubernetes/kubernetes repository (primarily under staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/ which is also vendored from the apiserver module).\\n\\n## Core Admission Infrastructure\\n\\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/interfaces.go`** defines the foundational interfaces:\\n- `Interface`: base interface with `Handles(operation Operation) bool`\\n- `MutationInterface`: extends Interface with `Admit(ctx, a Attributes, o ObjectInterfaces) error` for mutating plugins\\n- `ValidationInterface`: extends Interface with `Validate(ctx, a Attributes, o ObjectInterfaces) error` for validating plugins\\n- `Attributes`: carries all request context (resource, operation, object, user, etc.)\\n- `PluginInitializer`: initializes plugins with shared resources\\n- `ReinvocationContext`: tracks reinvocation state for re-invocation policy\\n\\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/attributes.go`** implements `attributesRecord` (the concrete `Attributes`), created via `NewAttributesRecord()`.\\n\\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/handler.go`** provides `Handler`, the embeddable base struct for admission plugins implementing operation filtering and readiness.\\n\\n## Plugin Registration\\n\\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugins.go`** provides `Plugins` registry:\\n- `Register(name, Factory)`: registers a plugin factory\\n- `NewFromPlugins(pluginNames, configProvider, initializer, decorator)`: creates the full chain in order, returning a `reinvocationHandler` wrapping a `chainAdmissionHandler`\\n- `InitPlugin(name, config, initializer)`: instantiates and initializes one plugin\\n\\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/plugins.go`** - `RegisterAllAdmissionPlugins()` registers the generic built-in plugins (NamespaceLifecycle, MutatingAdmissionWebhook, ValidatingAdmissionWebhook, MutatingAdmissionPolicy, ValidatingAdmissionPolicy).\\n\\n**`pkg/kubeapiserver/options/plugins.go`** - kube-apiserver's `RegisterAllAdmissionPlugins()` registers all kube-specific plugins and defines `AllOrderedPlugins` which specifies the canonical ordering of all plugins (mutating before validating, with webhook plugins near the end).\\n\\n## Admission Chain Execution\\n\\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/chain.go`** implements `chainAdmissionHandler` (a `[]Interface`) which iterates through all plugins:\\n- `Admit()`: calls `MutationInterface.Admit()` for each plugin that handles the operation\\n- `Validate()`: calls `ValidationInterface.Validate()` for each plugin that handles the operation\\n\\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/reinvocation.go`** wraps the chain with `reinvoker`:\\n- `Admit()`: runs the chain once, then if `ShouldReinvoke()` is true, runs it a second time (re-invocation policy)\\n- This is how mutating admission plugins get a second chance when a later plugin mutates the object\\n\\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/audit.go`** - `WithAudit()` wraps the chain to log audit annotations after Admit/Validate calls.\\n\\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/decorator.go`** - `Decorators` applies a list of `Decorator`s around each plugin (e.g., metrics instrumentation).\\n\\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/metrics/metrics.go`** - `WithControllerMetrics` decorates each named plugin, `WithStepMetrics` decorates the entire chain.\\n\\n## Mutating Admission Ordering\\n\\nThe `AllOrderedPlugins` list in `pkg/kubeapiserver/options/plugins.go` defines that all mutating plugins (in-tree controllers + MutatingAdmissionPolicy + MutatingAdmissionWebhook) run before all validating plugins (ValidatingAdmissionPolicy + ValidatingAdmissionWebhook). The `chainAdmissionHandler` respects this by calling `Admit()` only on `MutationInterface` implementors and `Validate()` only on `ValidationInterface` implementors in order. The `reinvoker` enables the re-invocation policy where webhooks with `IfNeeded` policy can be called again if subsequent plugins mutate the object.\\n\\n## Mutating Webhook Admission\\n\\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/plugin.go`**: `Plugin` implements `admission.MutationInterface`. `Register()` registers it as `MutatingAdmissionWebhook`. `Admit()` calls `a.Webhook.Dispatch()`.\\n\\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/generic/webhook.go`**: `Webhook` base struct shared by mutating and validating webhook plugins. `Dispatch()` checks if ready, fetches webhooks from `hookSource`, then calls `dispatcher.Dispatch()`. `ShouldCallHook()` checks namespace selector, object selector, and rules matching.\\n\\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/dispatcher.go`**: `mutatingDispatcher.Dispatch()` iterates webhooks in order (sequentially, not in parallel), checks re-invocation context, calls `callAttrMutatingHook()` which makes the HTTP call to the webhook, applies the returned JSON patch to the object, and marks the context for reinvocation if mutations occurred.\\n\\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/reinvocationcontext.go`**: `webhookReinvokeContext` tracks which webhooks have been invoked and should be re-invoked.\\n\\n## Validating Webhook Admission\\n\\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/plugin.go`**: `Plugin` implements `admission.ValidationInterface`.
